###SOL Rework, The Solar Age, new focuses###
###Damn you, EQS spaghetti code###
###Coded by Test4Echo###

###Sunset joins in on the evil fun###
shared_focus = {
    id = SOL_sunset_awaken
    icon = GFX_goal_sunrise_sparkle
    x = 6
    y = -1

    cost = 10
    allow_branch = {
		is_EQS_SOL = yes
		has_country_flag = SOL_unlock_political_focuses
	}
    available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOL_has_captured_sunset
			}
			has_country_flag = SOL_has_captured_sunset
		}
		else = {
			has_country_flag = SOL_captured_element_bearers
		}
        OR = {
            has_completed_focus = SOL_empress_protector
            has_completed_focus = SOL_empress_mother
            has_completed_focus = SOL_god_empress
        }
    }
    select_effect = {
        hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = solarreworked.205
				days = 20
			}
			country_event = {
				id = solarreworked.206
				days = 43
			}
			country_event = {
				id = solarreworked.207
				days = 68
			}
        }
    }
    completion_reward = {
        log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_sunset_awaken"
        set_global_flag = SOL_sunset_converted
        set_country_flag = SOL_sunset_ascended
        country_event = solarreworked.208
        if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SOL_solaris_adoratio
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = solarreworked.301
					days = 90
					random_days = 45
				}
			}
        }
    }
    ai_will_do = {
        base = 150
        modifier = {
            has_completed_focus = SOL_twilight_ascend
            add = 150
        }
    }
}

###Tweaked checks for Sunrise focus###
shared_focus = {
	id = SOL_twilight_ascend
	icon = GFX_goal_sunrise_sparkle
	cost = 10
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 300
	}
	x = 4
	y = -1
	allow_branch = {
		is_EQS_SOL = yes
		has_country_flag = SOL_unlock_political_focuses
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOL_has_twilight
			}
			has_country_flag = SOL_has_twilight
		}
		else = {
			has_country_flag = SOL_captured_element_bearers
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = SOL_empress_protector
			has_completed_focus = SOL_empress_mother
			has_completed_focus = SOL_god_empress
		}
	}
	select_effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = solarempire.46
				days = 15
			}
			country_event = {
				id = solarempire.47
				days = 35
			}
			country_event = {
				id = solarempire.48
				days = 68
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_twilight_ascend"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = SOL_twilight_converted
			if = {
				limit = {
					CRY = {
						has_country_leader = { character = EQS_twilight_sparkle ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { ROOT.crysparkle = CRY }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { ROOT.crysparkle = ROOT }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = crysparkle
				}
				var:crysparkle = {
					EQS_twilight_sparkle = {
						set_character_flag = twilight_char_ascended_flag
						set_character_name = EQS_SOL_evil_twilight_sparkle
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/EQS/Sunrise_Sparkle_new.tga"
								small = "GFX_idea_evil_twilight_sparkle"
							}
							army = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/EQS/Sunrise_Sparkle_new.tga"
								small = "GFX_idea_evil_twilight_sparkle"

							}
						}
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = no

							country_leader = {
								expire = "1965.1.1"
								ideology = falangism
								traits = {
									lady_inquisitor
								}
							}
						}
						remove_advisor_role = {
							slot = political_advisor
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { var:crysparkle = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } } }
					var:crysparkle = {
						# workaround for set_autonomy resetting controller
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { is_controlled_by = PREV }
							}
							set_variable = { CRY_controller = this.controller }
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = SOL_twilight_governor
					set_autonomy = { target = var:crysparkle autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat }
					var:crysparkle = {
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								has_variable = CRY_controller
							}
							var:CRY_controller = { set_state_controller = PREV }
							clear_variable = CRY_controller
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = CRY_SOL
						add_autonomy_ratio = { value = -0.20 }
						set_country_flag = CRY_solar_governorship
						set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = EQS_SOL_fascism_party_long name = EQS_SOL_fascism_party }
						EQS_twilight_sparkle = {
							promote_character = falangism
						}
						load_focus_tree = crystal_empire_solar_focus

						if = {
							limit = {
								has_character = CRY_shining_armour
								CRY_shining_armour = { is_unit_leader = yes }
							}
							remove_unit_leader_role = CRY_shining_armour
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clear_variable = crysparkle
		}
		country_event = solarempire.13
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SOL_solaris_inquisitionis
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = solarreworked.302
					days = 90
					random_days = 45
				}
			}
        }
	}
}

###New civil war focuses###
shared_focus = {
	id = SOL_civil_war_measures
	icon = GFX_goal_solar_military_factory
	cost = 5
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 300
	}
	x = 18
	y = -1
	available = {
		eqs_has_civil_war = yes
	}
	allow_branch = {
		is_EQS_SOL = yes
	}
	bypass = {
		eqs_has_civil_war = no
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = equestrian_civil_war_ended
			has_global_flag = equestrian_com_civil_war_ended
			has_global_flag = equestrian_civil_war_daybreaker_ended
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NLR
			}
			NLR = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = event_target:equestria
			}
			event_target:equestria = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			is_subject = no
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_civil_war_measures"
		###Event of Daybreaker passing the war measures act, which gets thundrous applause, aside from a few, as they see democracy die
		add_ideas = SOL_civil_war_measures_idea
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS FOCUS_FILTER_RESISTANCE FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}

shared_focus = {
	id = SOL_reconquer_equestria
	icon = GFX_goal_solar_unite_equestria
	relative_position_id = SOL_take_everypony
	prerequisite = {
		focus = SOL_herald_doom
		focus = SOL_take_everypony
		focus = SOL_counter_terrorists
	}
	available = {
		is_subject = no
	}
	bypass = {
		all_of = {
			array = core_states
			var:v = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						NOT = {
							is_eqs_civil_war_tag = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = SCS
	will_lead_to_war_with = LSP
	will_lead_to_war_with = BUF
	will_lead_to_war_with = NLR
	will_lead_to_war_with = NMS
	will_lead_to_war_with = CES
	will_lead_to_war_with = VAN
	will_lead_to_war_with = BAL
	will_lead_to_war_with = JUN
	cost = 7
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 50
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	x = 0
	y = 1
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_reconquer_equestria"
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_eqs_civil_war_tag = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUF = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = BUF
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = eqs_civil_war_victory
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 6023
			name = EQS_SOL_invicta_vp
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION }
}

###New Politics! We love Democracy###

    id = SOL_waking_dawn_star

    x = 10
    y = -1
    available = {
		is_subject = no
		has_DB_ruler = yes
	}
	cost = 1
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 200
		modifier = {
            has_war_with = CHN
            factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
            has_completed_focus = SOL_civil_war_measures
            factor = 3
		}
	}
	allow_branch = {
		is_EQS_SOL = yes
	}
	completion_reward = {
        ###Event of Daybreaker revealing herself to the Canterlot, and she is initially attacked by some of her own soldiers, who she deals with as she proclaims that she will lead the nation to greatness and destruction of the changelings; she is passive until she's shot at
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_waking_dawn_star"
		country_event = solarreworked.20
	}
}

    id = SOL_appoint_committee

			}

        log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus SOL_appoint_committee"
        add_ideas = SOL_imperial_war_committee
    }

shared_focus = {
    id = SOL_answer_crimes
    x = 0
    y = 1
    relative_position_id = SOL_fire_ministers

    cost = 3
    prerequisite = { focus = SOL_fire_ministers }
    available = {
        is_subject = no
        has_DB_ruler = yes
    }
    available = {
        is_subject = no
        has_DB_ruler = yes
        if = {
			limit = {
				has_power_balance = { id = EQS_vestments_of_power_bop }
				is_ai = no
